Implementation Highlights. The supplementary courses must be completed at the latest before applying for the degree oral defense. If you have not completed this course, you are not allowed to apply for the oral defense.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

Course enrollment must comply with university’s Regulations for Intercollegiate Course Selection and related provisions.</p><p>3.Courses under the <em>Joint Doctoral Training Program in Business and Management in Taiwan</em> must be approved by the program convener of the student’s major before they can be counted as elective credits in either the Special Topic category or Methods category.</p></td></tr></table>

```markdown
**Yuan Ze University, College of Management
Doctor of Philosophy Program Study Guide**
(For Foreign students, entrance in academic year 105)

105.04.20 Passed by the fifth academic affairs meeting of the 104th academic year

106.06.21 Revised and approved at the sixth academic meeting of the 105th academic year

107.01.10 Revised and approved at the third academic meeting of the 106th academic year

108.01.02 Revised and approved at the fourth academic meeting of the 107th academic year

108.05.01 The sixth academic affairs meeting of the 107th academic year revised and approved

109.05.06 Revised and approved at the sixth academic meeting of the 108th academic year

110. 01.06 Revised and approved at the third academic meeting of the 109th academic year

111.11.16 Passed by the second academic meeting of the academic year 111.11.16

112.05.31 Revised and adopted at the seventh academic meeting of the 111 academic year

1. **General rules**

a.	The guide is written according to the “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Master and Doctoral Degree Qualifying Examination.”

b. 	College of Management’s Doctor of Philosophy program (hereinafter Ph.D. program) consists of management group, finance group, and accounting group.

2. **Length of study years and school regulation for credits**

a.	The study length of years for a doctoral program is 2-7 years.

b.	School regulation for credits and compulsory/ elective courses.

1.	Students of the Ph.D. program need to complete a minimum of 30 credits and a doctoral dissertation.

2.	The courses of Ph.D. program include:

i.	Basic Compulsory Courses (3 credits): Business Research Methods

ii.	Other Compulsory Courses (6 credits):

<table><tr><td><p>Group</p></td><td><p>Required subjects</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Management</p></td><td><p>Strategy Theory and Management</p><p>Organization Theory and Management</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><p>Individual economic analysis</p><p>econometrics</p></td></tr></table>

1. Other elective subjects : Please refer to the list of elective subjects stipulated in the doctoral program . Doctoral students in the management group are required to apply for a supervisor within one week of the start of the third semester after enrollment , and submit a letter of intent to select courses with the consent of the supervisor. For non-listed management-related fields, a list of elective subjects must be proposed with the consent of the instructor or thesis advisor and submitted to the class meeting for approval before implementation .
2. Prerequisite subjects:

prerequisite courses must be submitted one week before the start of the semester, but the course will not be included in graduation credits.

<table><tr><td><p>Group</p></td><td><p>Prerequisite subjects</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><p>Quantitative methods, financial management</p></td></tr></table>

1. Doctoral students within the first two years of study should take the special seminar courses offered by the class. This course is not included in the graduation program.

points and present the paper at least once in a seminar course before the thesis oral examination.

Chapter 1 Qualifying exam

E. " Qualifying Examination/Thesis Proposal Application Form " (Appendix 1) within the specified time and pass the following examinations:

<table><tr><td colspan="3"><p>Qualification Examination Key Points</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Group</p></td><td><p>Exam time</p></td><td><p>Qualifying Examination Subjects</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Management</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>Held at least once every semester</p><p>(Held one week before the start of each semester)</p></td><td><p>social science research methods</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><p>financial research methods</p><p>econometrics</p><p>social science research methods</p><p>( Choose one from three ) </p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Note</p></td><td colspan="2"><ol><li>The qualification examination (including make-up exams) must be passed within four years of study. Those who fail to pass will be dropped from school.</li><li>The passing score for the qualification examination is 70 points or above (including 70 points).</li><li>Those who fail the qualification exam must make up the exam, no matter the subject , it is limited to one time . Those who fail the make-up exam will be dropped from school. The make-up exam time will be notified later.</li><li>An application to cancel the exam before the qualification exam is deemed to have failed the qualification exam. If you are unable to come to the exam due to force majeure, you need to submit a cancellation application one week before the exam date. If you are unable to submit a cancellation application as scheduled due to major reasons, you can make a supplementary application within one week after the exam date, and after it is approved by the class meeting, the cancellation application will not be considered. If you fail, the number of applications is limited to once.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

Chapter 4 PhD thesis

- Application for thesis advisor

Doctoral students are required to fill out the "Thesis Supervision Professor Application Form" (Appendix 2) in their research field within one week of the start of the third semester after admission to apply for one or more thesis supervisors to co-supervise the doctoral class. The supervisor should be Full-time teachers in this group will be given priority. If they are not full-time teachers in this group or need to find external teachers for joint guidance, they must be submitted to the class meeting for approval with the consent of the convener of the group . Before a doctoral student has selected a supervisor, the doctoral class will assign a full-time faculty member of the school to serve as a supervisor to guide his/her course work. After the doctoral candidate selects a topic, he or she will write the thesis plan under the guidance of the thesis advisor.

- Change of advisor

The application for changing the supervisor must be separated by one semester from the application for thesis supervisor, that is, the application cannot be submitted in the same semester. Doctoral students should fill out the "Application Form for Changing Thesis Advisor" (Appendix 3) and submit a letter of consent from the original thesis advisor and the new advisor. The change will be approved by the class meeting. The change of thesis advisor cannot be in the same semester as the submission of the thesis proposal oral examination and thesis oral examination application, and the change of thesis advisor must be done once and must be approved by the class meeting . If a doctoral student fails to change the advisor without complying with the regulations, Their degree examination results will not be recognized.

- Termination of mentoring relationship

If the mentoring relationship needs to be terminated for any reason, the instructor or student can take the initiative to apply in accordance with the regulations, and the application will be discussed and approved at the class meeting. After passing, students need to re-apply to the advisor.

- Thesis Examination Committee

Doctoral students began to apply for thesis examination in their third year of study and formed a thesis examination committee. This committee is responsible for the oral examination of the dissertation. The committee members are nominated by the supervisor and are composed of five to nine scholars in related fields with the approval of the convener of the group and the head teacher of the doctoral class. Among them, professors or associate professors should account for at least half of the committee, and external members should account for at least half of the thesis examination committee. After deducting the supervisor, there should be at least one teacher in the group . During the examination, the committee will recommend one person to serve as chairman. If the list of examination committee members changes, it must be resubmitted to the "Roster of Thesis Examination Committee" (Appendix 4) for related matters.

Anyone who is a third-degree relative or significant stakeholder of a doctoral student shall voluntarily withdraw from serving as the student's supervisor or thesis examination committee member. If found, his/her qualifications will be revoked. If the oral examination has been completed, the results of the oral examination will be invalid . If it is discovered that a doctorate degree has been awarded, the degree will be revoked and the issued degree certificate will be recovered.

- Thesis proposal oral examination

When applying, you should fill in (1) Thesis Proposal Oral Examination Application Form (Appendix 1) , (2) Thesis Examination Committee List (Appendix 4) , (3) Previous Transcripts and (4) Thesis Proposal Oral Examination Checklist ( Attachment 7) , with the consent of the supervisor and the convener of the group , submit it to the class meeting for review. <u>The oral examination shall be attended by members of the school's thesis examination committee._</u>The score of the oral examination is 70% for passing and 100% for full score. The score is determined by the average of the scores of the attending committee members. Those who fail the oral examination may apply to take it again in the next semester, but only once. If you pass the thesis proposal oral examination and take a leave of absence during the semester, you will need to reapply after resuming school and take another thesis proposal oral examination.

- Research results published

- Students are required to co-author a paper with their supervisor, the research institution is Yuanze University, and the paper must be published during their studies in this doctoral program.
- 6 or above meets the requirements for publication of research results.
- The connotation of all relevant results published must be consistent with the field of management expertise, and must be reviewed and approved by the supervisor before submission. The scope of " Other English journals with anonymous review system (and their counting) " and "Other international or domestic academic seminars ( and their counting )" must be approved by the convener of each group in advance and approved by the class meeting for future reference .

- Seminars must be published in the form of oral reports , international seminar papers must be published in English , and the applicant must be the presenter. If there are other doctoral students who co-authored the paper, you need to fill in the application form for graduation research points for the seminar paper. Only with the signatures and consent of all co-authored doctoral students can the seminar paper be counted as graduation research points.
- If the content of different results published has high overlap , it will be reviewed and decided by the class meeting , and the higher point will be scored once.
- Definition of Journal Article B:

1. Co-authored by one to four people ( at least one of them must be an assistant professor or above in our school ) , counted as one article .
2. For co-authors of five to seven people ( at least three of whom must be assistant professors or above, at least two of whom must be assistant professors or above in our school ) , the calculation is based on 0.5 articles .
3. eight or more people: not counted.
4. For papers co-authored by two or more students, the points will be calculated based on the average method.

- Dissertation oral examination

Doctoral students applying for the doctoral thesis oral examination should apply within the time specified in the calendar. When applying, they should submit (1) the first draft of the thesis, (2) the recommendation letter from the supervisor (Attachment 5) and (3) the graduation thesis oral examination checklist (Attachment ) 8) Then report it to the school for verification. The oral examination score is 70% for passing and 100% for full score. The score of the doctoral thesis oral examination is determined by the average of the scores of the attending committee members. Those who fail the oral examination may apply to take it again in the next semester, but only once.

who has taken 申請the doctoral degree examination is unable to complete the degree examination within that semester for any reason, he or she must fill out the "Degree Examination Cancellation Application Form" 應於本(Appendix 6) before the oral examination deadline specified by the doctoral class to apply for cancellation of the degree examination for that semester. Application for degree oral examination is limited to one time. Those who fail to withdraw or take the exam after the expiry date will be deemed to have failed once.

A doctoral student who has reached the last year of study and is eligible to apply for an oral examination but still cannot obtain the consent of his or her supervisor to conduct a dissertation oral examination may 向本appeal to the doctoral class.

If plagiarism or fraud is discovered in a doctoral degree awarded by this doctoral program, and if it is found to be true after investigation, the degree will be revoked and the issued degree certificate will be recovered.

```markdown
**Yuan Ze University, College of Management
Doctor of Philosophy Program Study Guide**
(For Foreign students, entrance in academic year 106)

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on January 03, 2024

1. **General rules**

a.	The guide is written according to the “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Master and Doctoral Degree Qualifying Examination.”

b. 	College of Management’s Doctor of Philosophy program (hereinafter Ph.D. program) consists of management group, finance group, and accounting group.

2. **Length of study years and school regulation for credits**

a.	The study length of years for a doctoral program is 2-7 years.

b.	School regulation for credits and compulsory/ elective courses.

1.	Students of the Ph.D. program need to complete a minimum of 30 credits and a doctoral dissertation.

2.	The courses of Ph.D. program include:

i.	Basic Compulsory Courses (3 credits): Business Research Methods

ii.	Other Compulsory Courses (6 credits):

<table><tr><td><p>Group</p></td><td><p>Compulsory Courses</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Management</p></td><td><ul><li>Strategy Management</li><li>Organization Behavior</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><ul><li>Economic Analysis</li><li>Econometrics</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><p>Accounting</p></td><td><ul><li>Microeconomic Analysis</li><li>Econometrics</li></ul></td></tr></table>

iii.	Research Method Courses (3 credits): Students are required to take one of the research method and analysis courses appointed by their major groups. This course is considered one of the courses in the Qualifying Examination. The analysis courses appointed by each major group are shown below:

<table><thead><tr><th><p>Group</p></th><th><p>Research Method Courses</p></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><p>Management</p></td><td><p>Marketing Research</p><p>Advanced Research Method</p><p>Multivariate Data Analysis (Choose 1 from 3)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><p>Empirical Finance</p><p>Advanced Research Method </p><p>Multivariate Data Analysis (Choose 1 from 3)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Accounting</p></td><td><p>Empirical Finance</p><p>Advanced Research Method </p><p>Multivariate Data Analysis (Choose 1 from 3)</p></td></tr></tbody></table>

iv.	Other Elective Courses: please refer to the list of required courses provided by the Doctor of Philosophy program. Finance major students in the Ph.D. program need to accomplish five compulsory courses. Management-related area which is not on the list need to provide the Course Sign Up Form approved by the dissertation advisor or instructor and sent to the Affair Council to be decided.

v.	Prerequisite Courses:

Students need to apply for the prerequisite courses waived at least one week before the starting date of each academic semester. The prerequisite courses are not included in the graduation credits.

<table><tr><td><p>Group</p></td><td><p>Prerequisite Courses</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance </p></td><td><p>Quantitative Methods, Financial Management</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Accounting</p></td><td><p>Intermediate Accounting (6 Credits Min), Cost or Management Accounting (6 Credits Min), and Auditing (6 Credits Min)</p></td></tr></table>

3.	Students have to take Seminar in Management (Management group) and Special Topics on Corporate Finance, Special Topics on Investment Management, and Seminar in Management (Finance group) courses within the first two years when starting the Ph.D. study and such courses are not included in the graduation credits. In addition, students should hold an academic speech at least once in the Special Topics or Seminar before the doctoral oral defense.

**C. 	Examination**

Ph.D. students need to submit the "Notification of Learning Process" (including Qualifying Examination/ Dissertation Proposal, Attachment 1) by a certain period of time and pass the examinations listed below:

<table><tr><td colspan="3"><p>Qualifying Examination</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Group</p></td><td><p>Time Table</p></td><td><p>Qualifying Examination Subject</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Management</p></td><td rowspan="3"><p>Held at least once per semester (a week before the starting date of the semester)</p></td><td><p>Business Research Methods</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><p>Empirical Finance, <br/>Econometrics, </p><p>Business Research Methods<br/>(Choose 1 from 3)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Accounting</p></td><td><p>Financial Accounting Theory</p><p>Advanced Managerial Accounting</p><p>Advanced Auditing</p><p>(Choose 1 from 3)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="2"><ol><li>The passing grade for qualifying examination is 70 (including 70).</li><li>Students who fail the qualifying examination are required to retake the exam once only regardless of which course. The timetable of the retaken examination will be scheduled upon need.</li><li>Any withdrawal request of the qualifying examination before exam scheduled dates will be considered as a failure of this qualifying examination.</li><li>Student who needs to withdraw qualifying examination due to unavoidable matters should apply a week earlier before examination date. Student who cannot meet this requirement due to a major incident can submit an examination retake application one week later, and the failure record may be canceled after the committee meeting. But apply one time only.</li><li>Students who published to top class international journals are qualified to wave the qualification exam, the notes are as follow :</li></ol><p>(1)The journal paper should be SSCI, SCI, or TSSCI.</p><p>(2)The journal paper should be published after enrolling Ph.D. program in Yuan Ze University, and published in the name of Yuan Ze University with one specially appointed professor as co-author. </p><p>(3)The journal paper could only be applied by one Ph.D. student, and this paper would not be counted as research points for graduation. </p><p>(4)Students should prepare the application form “Application for Ph.D. Qualifying Examination Waive” as attachment 11, the journal accepted letter (published paper won’t have to be submitted), abstract of the paper, and the referral of the journal to the office. </p><p>(5)Qualification exam should be completed within four years of enrollment.</p></td></tr></table>

**D. Dissertation**

1. Dissertation Advisor

Ph.D. students need to apply for the acceptance of the dissertation advisor within the first week of their 3<sup>rd</sup> semester (Application for Dissertation Advisor form, attachment 2). Students may apply for one advisor or above to provide instruction together, one of them should be participating faculty in the group in which students major. Students must acquire the consent of the coordinator of the major group, if the advisor is not the faculty in the student's major group or the co-advisor is not a faculty of the College of Management, YZU. Before the finalization of the advisor issue, the Ph.D. program will indicate one participating faculty as the mentor of students for study advising. Doctor candidates need to decide on the topic and then start to draft the dissertation under the instruction of an advisor.

2. Change of Advisor

There should be a semester as an interval between the time to apply change of dissertation advisor and the time to apply for acceptance of the dissertation advisor. Also, the time to apply for a change of dissertation advisor will not be allowed in the same semester with the application for acceptance. Students need to fill out the form “Application for Changing Dissertation Advisor” as attachment 3 and provide the agreements from both previous and current advisors as necessary documents for Ph.D. program committee meetings. It is not allowed to change advisors in the same semester as they apply for dissertation proposal defense and dissertation oral defense. The limitation of change advisor is only one time during the Ph.D. study period. The grade of the dissertation oral defense will not be recognized if the students do not follow the procedure of changing dissertation advisor.

3. Dissertation Committee

Students may apply for the dissertation oral defense and constitute the dissertation committee since the 5<sup>th</sup> semester of the program. The dissertation committee is in charge of reviewing the dissertation oral defense. After the consent of the dissertation advisor and Ph.D. program director of the committee members, there will be five to nine scholars in the related fields to constitute the committee. Above 50% of the committee members are professors or associate professors, and above 50% of the committee members are faculty from other universities than YZU. Except for the dissertation committee, there should be one faculty from the candidate's major group in the committee, and there will be a chairperson nominated by the committee to coordinate issues. The form “List of Dissertation Committee Members” as attachment 4 is a document to keep a record of committee members for the program. Any change of the list needs to be updated as soon as the validation of the change.

Students should exclude their three degrees of kinships or stakeholders as their dissertation advisors or committee members; otherwise, the qualification shall be revoked and the grades of oral defense shall not be recognized by the program. If the program confers a degree to a student who is found to do so, the program shall revoke the degree and issue a public notice to announce the invalidation of the previously issued diploma.

4. Dissertation Proposal Defense

The application documents need to be approved by dissertation advisors and the coordinator of the student's major group and approved for reference in the Ph.D. Program Committee meeting. The application documents include:

- Notification of Learning Process (as Attachment 1)
- List of Dissertation Committee Members (as Attachment 4)
- Transcript of Ph.D. program
- Checklist for Applying Dissertation Proposal Defense (as Attachment 7)

The Dissertation Proposal Defense will be attended by the Dissertation Committee members in the school. The committee members will work out an average score. The passing score is 70 out of 100. Students who fail the proposal defense may apply for another proposal defense in the next semester with a limitation of a one-time chance. The Dissertation Proposal Defense and Dissertation Oral Defense should not be in the same semester.

5. Articles Published

Ph.D. students must meet the below articles' published requirements prior to obtaining a Ph.D. degree:

1.	Students must coauthor with dissertation advisors and must state Yuan Ze University as the research institution in the articles and the article needs to be published while attending school.

2.	Students need to achieve a minimum of 6 points in order to meet the article's published requirement. Except for those who are in their last year (the 7<sup>th</sup> year), students in Management majors take SSCI, SCI, and TSSCI journals only, and students in Finance and Accounting majors take Level <strong>III</strong> journals defined by the College of Management, YZU.

3.	All research categories of the published articles should be relevant to the management professional field and the article needs to be audited and get approval from the advisor before submitting for publication. The list of other anonymous peer review journals (and the points students can have), average-class international conferences, and domestic conferences should be reviewed by the coordinator of each group in advance and approved for reference in the Ph.D. program committee meeting (attachment 9).

<table><tr><td colspan="2"><p><a></a>Types of Publication</p></td><td><p>Points</p></td><td><p>Remarks</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="4"><p>i. One journal paper (published or accepted)</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>SSCI class journals</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td rowspan="6"></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>SCI class journals</p></td><td><p>8</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>TSSCI class journals</p></td><td><p>6</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>FLI class journals</p></td><td><p>6</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Lever II journals defined by each discipline</p></td><td><p>8</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Lever III journals defined by each discipline</p></td><td><p>6</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Other anonymous peer-reviewed journals</p></td><td><p>3-4</p></td><td><p>Case-by-case review</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="4"><p>ii. One paper published in the conference</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Top-class international conference</p></td><td><p>6</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>Listed below</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Excellent class international conference</p></td><td><p>4</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Average-class international conference</p></td><td><p>1-2</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>Case-by-case review and cannot exceed 2 points in total point</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Domestic Conference</p></td><td><p>1-2</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="4"><p>iii. One published case study </p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Harvard Business School Publishing</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Ivey Publishing, Richard Ivey School of Business Foundation</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Kung-Hwa Management Cases Collections</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>Cannot exceed 4 points in total point</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Taiwan Management Case Center</p></td><td><p>2</p></td></tr></table>

4. The list of top-class international conferences is below:

<table><tr><td><p>Group</p></td><td><p>Top-class international conference</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Management </p></td><td><ul><li>Academy of Management (AOM) Annual Meeting </li><li>ACR North American Conference </li><li>International Conference on Information Systems (ICIS)</li><li>American Finance Association Annual Meeting/American Economic Association Annual Meeting (AFA/AEA)</li><li>Western Finance Association Annual Meeting (WFA)</li><li>Financial Management Association Annual Meeting (FMA)</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><ul><li>American Finance Association Annual Meeting/American Economic Association Annual Meeting (AFA/AEA)</li><li>Western Finance Association Annual Meeting (WFA)</li><li>Financial Management Association Annual Meeting (FMA)</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><p>Accounting</p></td><td><ul><li>AAA Annual Meeting</li><li>AAA Regional Meeting</li><li>AAA Section Meeting</li><li>Financial Management Association Annual Meeting (FMA)</li><li>American Finance Association Annual Meeting/American Economic Association Annual Meeting (AFA/AEA)</li></ul></td></tr></table>

5. The list of excellent international conferences is below:

<table><thead><tr><th><p>Group</p></th><th><p>Excellent class international conference </p></th></tr><tr><th><p>Management</p></th><th><ul><li>Academy of Human Resource Development Annual Meeting </li><li>Asia Academy of Management Annual Meeting (AAOM) </li><li>Australia and New Zealand International Business Academy (ANZIBA) Annual Conference</li><li>Australian and New Zealand Academy of Management Conference (ANZAM) </li><li>British Academy of Management Conference (BAM) </li><li>Eastern Academy of Management Annual Meeting </li><li>EGOs Colloquium </li><li>European Association of Work and Organizational Psychology</li><li>International Labor and Employment Relations Association (ILERA) Asian Congress </li><li>International Labor and Employment Relations Association (ILERA) Biannual Congress</li><li>International Association for Chinese Management Research (IACMR) </li><li>International Association for Conflict Management (IACM) Annual Conference</li><li>International Conference on HRD Research and Practice Across Europe </li><li>Labor and Employment Relations Association (LERA) Annual Meeting  </li><li>Midwest Academy of Management Annual Meeting </li><li>Northeast Decision Sciences Institute Annual Conference (NEDSI) </li><li>Society for Industrial &amp; Organizational Psychology (SIOP) </li><li>Southwest Academy of Management Annual Meeting </li><li>Strategic Management Society Annual International Conference </li><li>The Academy of International Business (AIB) Annual Meeting </li><li>The European Academy of Management (EURAM) Annual Conference </li><li>American Marketing Association Conference </li><li>Academy of Marketing Science Conference </li><li>American Psychologist Association Conference</li><li>Asia-Pacific ACR Conference</li><li>European ACR Conference</li><li>Society of Consumer Psychology Conference</li><li>(ISPIM) International Society for Professional Innovation Management</li><li>(DSI) Decision Science Institute</li><li>(IAMOT) International Conference on Management of Technology</li><li>(AAA) American Academy of Advertising</li><li>Academy of International Business（AIB）</li><li>Strategic Management Society Conference(SMS)</li><li>EFA (European Finance Association Meeting) </li><li>EFMA (European Financial Management Association Meeting) </li><li>Financial Management Association (FMA) Asian Conference</li><li>Financial Management Association (FMA) European Conference </li><li>North American Meeting of the Econometric Society </li><li>European Meeting of the Econometric Society</li></ul></th></tr></thead></table>

<table><thead><tr><th></th><th><ul><li>Asian Meeting of the Econometric Society</li><li>SoFiE Annual Conference</li><li>International Symposium on Econometric Theory and Applications (SETA)</li><li>PICMET( Portland International Center for Management of Engineering and Technology)</li><li>Or other equivalent-quality international conference approved by finance group faculty</li></ul></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><ul><li>EFA (European Finance Association Meeting) </li><li>EFMA (European Financial Management Association Meeting) </li><li>Financial Management Association (FMA) Asian Conference</li><li>Financial Management Association (FMA) European Conference</li><li>North American Meeting of the Econometric Society Applications (SETA)</li><li>Or other equivalent-quality international conference approved by finance group faculty</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><p>Accounting </p></td><td><ul><li>The Congress of the Research Symposium (GMARS)</li><li>SoFiE Annual Conference</li><li>International Symposium on Econometric Theory and Applications (SETA)</li><li>Or other equivalent-quality international conference approved by finance group faculty</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table>

6.	Students should publish papers with oral presentations at conferences and should present in English at international conferences. Only the presenter's paper can be counted as a pointed publication. If there are any other Ph.D. students who co-write the paper with you, you would need to fill in the “Quitclaim of Co-authored Dissertation” as attachment 10 with all the co-author signatures on it.

7.	Similar content articles published in different conferences can only be counted in higher points once reviewed by program committee meetings.

8.	Definition of "one periodical article":

1. Articles with one to four authors (at least one of them must be an assistant professor or above in the College of Management, YZU) can be counted as one publication.
2. Articles with five to seven authors (at least three of them must be assistant professors or above and two of them must be assistant professors or above in the College of Management, YZU) can be counted as one-half publication only.
3. Articles with eight authors or above cannot be considered as pointed publications.
4. For Articles with two students or above as authors, the point will be counted on average.

6. Dissertation Oral Defense

Students should follow the procedure of the dissertation oral defense application along with the school calendar. The application documents include the following:

- Draft of dissertation
- Dissertation Recognition from Advisor (as Attachment 5)
- Checklist for Applying Dissertation Oral Defense (as Attachment 8)

The committee members will work out an average score. The passing score is 70 out of 100. Students who fail the oral defense may apply for another oral defense in the next semester with a limitation of a one-time chance.

Students who have already applied for dissertation oral defense but cannot execute the defense should submit a "Notification of Withdrawal of Application for Examination" (as Attachment 6) to withdraw the defense before the deadline for dissertation oral defense. The withdrawal of oral defense can only be applied for one time. Students who do not submit the form of “Notification of Withdrawal of Application for Examination” and do not execute the defense will be considered as a failure of the oral defense.

Students could appeal to the Ph.D. program when they reach the final year of the Ph.D. study period and are qualified to apply for oral defense but still cannot get the approval to execute the oral defense from their dissertation advisors.

In the event that the program confers a degree to a student who is found upon investigation to have committed plagiarism or used fraudulent means in preparing the dissertation, the program shall revoke the degree and issue a public notice to announce the invalidation of the previously issued diploma.

**E. 	Attachments**

Attachment 1: Notification of Learning Process

Attachment 2: Application for Dissertation Advisor

Attachment 3: Application for Changing Dissertation Advisor

Attachment 4: List of Dissertation Committee Members

Attachment 5: Dissertation Recognition from Advisor

Attachment 6: Notification of Withdrawal Application for Examination

Attachment 7: Checklist for Applying Dissertation Proposal Defense

Attachment 8: Checklist for Applying Dissertation Oral Defense

Attachment 9: Application for Unlisted Journal/ Conference Approval

Attachment10: Quitclaim of Co-authored Dissertation

Attachment 11: Application for Ph.D. Qualifying Examination Wave

**F. 	Supplementary**

```markdown
元智大學管理學院博士班修業要點

（107學年度入學學生適用）

107.05.02 一○六學年度第五次教務會議通過

107.06.27 一○六學年度第六次教務會議修訂通過

108.01.02 一○七學年度第四次教務會議修訂通過

108.05.01一○七學年度第六次教務會議修訂通過

109.05.06一○八學年度第六次教務會議修訂通過

110. 01.06 一○九學年度第三次教務會議修訂通過

111.11.16 一一一學年度第二次教務會議通過

112.05.31 一一一學年度第七次教務會議修訂通過

# 總則

### 本修業要點依元智大學碩、博士班研究生學位考試細則訂定之。

### 元智大學管理學院博士班(本要點稱本博士班)設有管理主修、財務金融主修及會計主修。

# 修業年限及學分規定

第三條   修業年限

博士班修業年限為二至七年。

第四條  學分數及必選修科目

- 博士生需在本博士班至少修滿三十學分及完成博士論文乙篇。
- 本班各主修修習之科目包括：

1. 基礎必修(3學分)：「社會科學研究方法」
2. 其他必修(6學分)：

<table><tr><td><p>主修</p></td><td><p>必選科目</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>管理</p></td><td><p>策略理論與管理</p><p>行為科學理論與管理</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>財務金融</p></td><td><p>個體經濟分析</p><p>計量經濟學</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>會計</p></td><td><p>個體經濟分析</p><p>計量經濟學</p></td></tr></table>

3.其它選修科目：請參照博士班修業規定之選修科目表。非表列之管理相關領域，需在導師或論文指導教授同意下，提出選修科目表，送班務會議通過後實施之。

4.先修科目：

先修科目於開學前一週提出抵免之申請，但該課程不列入畢業學分。

<table><tr><td><p>主修</p></td><td><p>先修科目</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>財務金融</p></td><td><p>數量方法、財務管理</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>會計</p></td><td><p>中級會計學(至少6學分)、成本會計或管理會計(至少6學分)、審計學(至少6學分)</p></td></tr></table>

- 博士班生於修業前二年內，應選修本班所開設之專題研討課程，該課程不列入畢業學分，並至少在學位論文口試前於專題研討課程中發表論文一次。

# 資格考試

- 修習本博士班課程應於規定時間填具「資格考試/論文計畫書申請表」(附件一)，並通過下列考試：

<table><tr><td colspan="3"><p>資格考試說明要點</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>主修</p></td><td><p>考試時間</p></td><td><p>資格考考試科目</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>管理</p></td><td rowspan="3"><p>每學期至少舉行一次</p><p>(每學期開學前一週舉行)</p></td><td><p>社會科學研究方法</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>財務金融</p></td><td><p>財務研究方法</p><p>計量經濟學</p><p>社會科學研究方法</p><p>(三選一) </p></td></tr><tr><td><p>會計</p></td><td><p>財務會計理論</p><p>高等管理會計學</p><p>高等審計學</p><p>(三選一)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p></td><td colspan="2"><ol><li>資格考試(含補考)須於在學四年內通過，未能通過者，予以退學。</li><li>資格考試的考試科目及格分數為70分以上(含70分)。</li><li>資格考試不及格者必須補考，不論科目以一次為限，補考未通過者，予以退學。補考時間另行通知。</li><li>在資格考試前提出撤銷考試之申請，即視同該次資格考試不及格。如因不可抗拒因素無法前來考試，需於考試日前一週提出撤銷申請，若遇重大事由無法如期提出撤銷申請，得於考試日後一週內補提申請，並經班務會議通過後，得不算不及格，但申請次數以一次為限。</li><li>學生於Ｉ級期刊發表可抵免資格考試，抵免注意事項如下:</li></ol><p>(1)申請抵免之期刊必須是SSCI、SCI、TSSCI期刊。</p><p>   (2)申請抵免之期刊論文必須是博士班入學後，以元智大學管理學院博士班名義發表，且需含本院專任教師為共同作者。</p><p>(3)申請抵免之期刊論文，每篇僅能被一名博士生申請抵免，且已抵免之論文不得採計畢業研究點數。</p><p>(4)學生應備妥申請表、論文接受函(已刊登者免)、論文摘要、期刊級別佐證資料向辦公室辦理申請。</p><p>(5)資格考試抵免需於在學四年內完成。</p></td></tr></table>

- 博士學位論文

- 論文指導教授之申請

博士生需於入學後第三學期開學一週內，就其研究領域填具「論文指導教授申請表」(附件二)向本博士班申請一位或多位論文指導教授共同指導，指導教授應以該主修專任教師為優先，若非該主修專任教師或需找校外老師共同指導，需經該主修召集人同意後報請班務會議核備。在博士生未選定指導教授前，由本博士班指派本院專任教師擔任導師，指導其課業。博士候選人選定題目後，在論文指導教授之指導下，進行論文計畫之寫作。

- 指導教授之變更

更換指導教授申請，需與提出論文指導教授申請間隔一學期，亦即不得在同一學期提出申請。博士生應填具「更換論文指導教授申請表」(附件三)辦理，並提出原論文指導教授與新的指導教授之同意書，經班務會議通過後變更。更換論文指導教授與提出論文計畫書口試及學位論文口試申請不能為同一學期，且更換論文指導教授以一次為原則，並需經班務會議通過，博士生未依規定逕自更換指導教授時，其學位考試成績不予承認。

- 指導關係之終止

若因故需終止指導關係，可由指導老師或學生方，依規定主動提出申請，並經班務會議討論通過。通過後學生需重新申請指導教授。

- 論文考試委員會

博士生得於博三上開始提出論文考試申請，並組成論文考試委員會。該委員會負責學位論文之口試，委員由指導教授提名並經該主修召集人及本博士班班主任同意後，聘請相關領域學者五至九人組成之。其中教授或副教授委員應至少佔委員會人數一半以上，校外委員至少佔論文考試委員會一半人數，且扣除指導教授後，應至少含該主修教師一名，考試時由委員會互推一人擔任主席。考試委員名單若有變動，需重新送交「論文考試委員會名冊」(附件四)辦理相關事宜。

為博士生三等親以內親屬或重大利害關係人，應自行迴避不得擔任該生之指導教授或論文考試委員，經發現者撤銷其資格，如已完成口試，則該次口試成績無效。已授予博士學位始發現時，則撤銷其學位，並追繳其已發之學位證書。

- 論文計畫書口試

申請時應填具(1)論文計畫書口試申請表(附件一)、(2)論文考試委員會名冊(附件四)、(3) 歷年成績單與(4)論文計畫書口試檢查表(附件七)，經指導教授及該主修召集人同意後報請班務會議核備。口試由該生論文考試委員會中之校內委員出席。口試成績以七十分為及格，一百分為滿分，以出席委員評定分數平均決定之。口試不及格者，得申請於次學期再次舉行，但以一次為限。論文計畫書口試與學位論文口試不能為同一學期。若通過論文計畫書口試當學期辦理休學，需於復學後重新申請，再進行一次論文計畫書口試。博七上學期結束前未通過論文計畫書口試者，予以退學。

- 研究成果發表

- 學生需與指導教授合著論文，研究機構為元智大學，並為就讀本博士班就學期間所發表。
- 6點以上即符合研究成果發表之要求。除修業年限最後一年（博七）的學生之外，畢業研究成果發表點數，僅採計期刊論文點。
- 所有相關成果發表之內涵須與管理專業領域契合，投稿前需先經指導教授審核並同意。「其他具匿名審查制之英文期刊（及其計點）」、「其他國際或國內學術研討會(及其計點)」之範圍，須事先申請由各主修召集人審定，並經班務會議備查。
- 頂尖國際研討會，會議名稱如下表。

- 研討會須以口頭報告方式發表，國際研討會論文須以英文發表，申請人需為發表人。若有其他博士生合著，需填寫研討會論文採計畢業研究點數申請表，經所有合著博士生簽名同意，方可採計為畢業研究點數。
- 不同成果發表之內涵，若重疊性高，由班務會議審查決定，以較高之點數計分一次。
- 期刊論文乙篇定義：

1. 一至四人合著(其中至少一人須為本院助理教授或以上)，以1篇計算。
2. 五至七人合著(至少三位為助理教授或以上，其中至少二人須為本院助理教授或以上)，以0.5篇計算。
3. 八人以上合著：不計入。
4. 兩位以上學生合著論文，其點數依平均方式計算。

- 學位論文口試

博士生申請博士學位論文口試，應依照行事曆規定時間內申請，申請時應檢齊(1)論文初稿、(2)指導教授推薦函(附件五)與(3)畢業論文口試檢查表(附件八)後報請學校核備。口試成績以七十分為及格，一百分為滿分。博士學位論文口試成績以出席委員評定分數平均決定之。口試不及格者，得申請於次學期再次舉行，但以一次為限。

已申請博士學位考試之博士生，若因故無法在該學期內完成學位考試，應於本博士班規定之口試截止日前填具「學位考試撤銷申請書」(附件六)報請撤銷該學期學位考試之申請，撤銷學位口試之申請以一次為限。逾期未撤銷亦未舉行考試者，以一次不及格論。

博士生已達修業年限最後一年且符合申請口試資格，仍無法獲得指導教授同意進行學位論文口試，可向本博士班提出申訴。

本博士班對已授予之博士學位，如發現論文有抄襲或舞弊情事，經調查屬實者，則撤銷其學位，並追繳其已發之學位證書。

**Yuan Ze University, College of Management
Doctor of Philosophy Program Study Guide**
(For Foreign Students, entrance in academic year 107)

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on January 03, 2024

1. **General rules**

a.	This guide is written according to the “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Master and Doctoral Degree Qualifying Examination.”

b. 	College of Management’s Doctor of Philosophy program (hereinafter Ph.D. program) consists of management group, finance group, and accounting group.

2. **Length of study years and school regulation for credits**

a.	The study length of years for a doctoral program is 2-7 years.

b.	School regulation for credits and compulsory/ elective courses.

1.	Students of the Ph.D. program need to complete a minimum of 30 credits and a doctoral dissertation.

2.	The courses of the Ph.D. program include:

i.	Basic Compulsory Courses (3 credits): Research Methodology for Social Sciences

ii.	Other Compulsory Courses (6 credits):

<table><tr><td><p>Group</p></td><td><p>Compulsory Courses</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Management</p></td><td><ul><li>Strategy Management</li><li>Organization Behavior</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><ul><li>Economic Analysis</li><li>Econometrics</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><p>Accounting</p></td><td><ul><li>Economic Analysis</li><li>Econometrics</li></ul></td></tr></table>

iii.	Other Elective Courses: please refer to the list of required courses provided by the Doctor of Philosophy program. Finance major students in the Ph.D. program need to accomplish five compulsory courses. Management-related area which is not on the list need to provide the Course Sign Up Form approved by the dissertation advisor or instructor and sent to the Affair Council to be decided.

iv.	Prerequisite Courses:

Students need to apply for the prerequisite courses waived at least one week before the starting date of each academic semester. The prerequisite courses are not included in the graduation credits.

<table><tr><td><p>Group</p></td><td><p>Prerequisite Courses</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance </p></td><td><p>Quantitative Methods, Financial Management</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Accounting</p></td><td><p>Intermediate Accounting (6 Credits Min), Cost or Management Accounting (6 Credits Min), and Auditing (6 Credits Min)</p></td></tr></table>

3.	Students have to take Seminar in Management (Management group) and Special Topics on Corporate Finance, Special Topics on Investment Management, and Seminar in Management (Finance group) courses within the first two years when starting the Ph.D. study and such courses are not included in the graduation credits. In addition, students should hold an academic speech at least once in the Special Topics or Seminar before the doctoral oral defense.

**C. 	Examination**

Ph.D. students need to submit the "Notification of Learning Process" (including Qualifying Examination/ Dissertation Proposal, Attachment 1) by a certain period of time and pass the examinations listed below:

<table><tr><td colspan="3"><p>Qualifying Examination</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Group</p></td><td><p>Time Table</p></td><td><p>Qualifying Examination Subject</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Management</p></td><td rowspan="3"><p>Held at least once per semester (a week before the starting date of the semester)</p></td><td><p>Research Methodology for Social Sciences</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><p>Empirical Finance, <br/>Econometrics, </p><p>Research Methodology for Social Sciences<br/>(Choose 1 from 3)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Accounting</p></td><td><p>Financial Accounting Theory</p><p>Advanced Managerial Accounting</p><p>Advanced Auditing</p><p>(Choose 1 from 3)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="2"><ol><li>The passing grade for the qualification exam is 70 (including 70).</li><li>Students who fail the qualifying examination must retake the exam only once regardless of which course. The timetable of the retaken examination will be scheduled upon need.</li><li>Any withdrawal request of the qualifying examination before the exam scheduled dates will be considered a failure of this qualifying examination.</li><li>Student who needs to withdraw qualifying examination due to unavoidable matters should apply a week before the examination date. Students who cannot meet this requirement due to a major incident can submit an examination retake application one week later, and the failure record may be canceled after the committee meeting. But apply one time only.</li><li>Students who publish in top-class international journals are qualified to waive the qualifying examination, the notes are as follows.</li></ol><p>(1)The journal paper should be SSCI, SCI, or TSSCI.</p><p>(2)The journal paper should be published after enrolling Ph.D. program in Yuan Ze University, and published in the name of Yuan Ze University with one specially appointed professor as co-author. </p><p>(3)The journal paper could only be applied by one Ph.D. student, and this paper would not be counted as research points for graduation. </p><p>(4)Students should prepare the application form “Application for Ph.D. Qualifying Examination Waive” as attachment 11, the journal accepted letter (published paper won’t have to be submitted), the abstract of the paper, and the referral of the journal to the office. </p><p>(5)Qualification exam should be completed within four years of enrollment.</p></td></tr></table>

**D. Dissertation**

1. Dissertation Advisor

Ph.D. students need to apply for the acceptance of the dissertation advisor within the first week of their 3<sup>rd</sup> semester (Application for Dissertation Advisor form, attachment 2). Students may apply for one advisor or above to provide instruction together, one of them should be participating faculty in the group in which students major. Students must acquire the consent of the coordinator of the major group, if the advisor is not the faculty in the student's major group or the co-advisor is not a faculty of the College of Management, YZU. Before the finalization of the advisor issue, the Ph.D. program will indicate one participating faculty as the mentor of students for study advising. Doctor candidates need to decide on the topic and then start to draft the dissertation under the instruction of an advisor.

2. Change of Advisor

There should be a semester as an interval between the time to apply change of dissertation advisor and the time to apply for acceptance of the dissertation advisor. Also, the time to apply for a change of dissertation advisor will not be allowed in the same semester with the application for acceptance. Students need to fill out the form “Application for Changing Dissertation Advisor” as attachment 3 and provide the agreements from both previous and current advisors as necessary documents for Ph.D. program committee meetings. It is not allowed to change dissertation advisors in the same semester as they apply for dissertation proposal defense and dissertation oral defense. The limitation of change advisor is only one time during the Ph.D. study period. The grade of the dissertation oral defense will not be recognized if the students do not follow the procedure of changing dissertation advisor.

3. Dissertation Committee

Students may apply for the dissertation oral defense and constitute the dissertation committee since the 5<sup>th</sup> semester of the program. The dissertation committee is in charge of reviewing the dissertation oral defense. After the consent of the advisor and Ph.D. program director of the committee members, there will be five to nine scholars in the related fields to constitute the committee. Above 50% of the committee members are professors or associate professors, and above 50% of the committee members are faculty from other universities than YZU. Except for the dissertation committee, there should be one faculty from the candidate's major group in the committee, and there will be a chairperson nominated by the committee to coordinate issues. The form “List of Dissertation Committee Members” as attachment 4 is a document to keep a record of committee members for the program. Any change of the list needs to be updated as soon as the validation of the change.

Students should exclude their three degrees of kinships or stakeholders as their dissertation advisors or committee members; otherwise, the qualification shall be revoked and the grades of oral defense shall not be recognized by the program. If the program confers a degree to a student who is found to do so, the program shall revoke the degree and issue a public notice to announce the invalidation of the previously issued diploma.

4. Dissertation Proposal Defense

The application documents need to be approved by dissertation advisors and the coordinator of the student's major group and approved for reference in the Ph.D. Program Committee meeting. The application documents include:

- Notification of Learning Process (as Attachment 1)
- List of Dissertation Committee Members (as Attachment 4)
- Transcript of Ph.D. program
- Checklist for Applying Dissertation Proposal Defense (as Attachment 7)

The Dissertation Proposal Defense will be attended by the Dissertation Committee members in the school. The committee members will work out an average score. The passing score is 70 out of 100. Students who fail the proposal defense may apply for another proposal defense next semester with a limitation of a one-time chance. The Dissertation Proposal Defense and Dissertation Oral Defense should not be in the same semester.

5. Articles Published

Ph.D. students must meet the below articles' published requirements prior to obtaining a Ph.D. degree:

1.	Students must coauthor with dissertation advisors and must state Yuan Ze University as the research institution in the articles and the article needs to be published while attending school.

2.	Students need to achieve a minimum of 6 points in order to meet the article's published requirement. Except for those who are in their last year (the 7<sup>th</sup> year), students in Management majors take SSCI, SCI, and TSSCI journals only, and students in Finance and Accounting majors take Level <strong>III</strong> journals defined by the College of Management, YZU.

3.	All research categories of the published articles should be relevant to the management professional field and the article needs to be audited and get approval from the dissertation advisor before submitting for publication. The list of other anonymous peer review journals (and the points students can have), average-class international conferences, and domestic conferences should be reviewed by the coordinator of each group in advance and approved for reference in the Ph.D. program committee meeting (attachment 9).

<table><tr><td colspan="2"><p><a></a>Types of Publication</p></td><td><p>Points</p></td><td><p>Remarks</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="4"><p>i. One journal paper (published or accepted)</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>SSCI class journals</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td rowspan="6"></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>SCI class journals</p></td><td><p>8</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>TSSCI class journals</p></td><td><p>6</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>FLI class journals</p></td><td><p>6</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Lever II journals defined by each discipline</p></td><td><p>8</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Lever III journals defined by each discipline</p></td><td><p>6</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Other anonymous peer review journals</p></td><td><p>3-4</p></td><td><p>Case-by-case review</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="4"><p>ii. One paper published in the conference</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Top-class international conference</p></td><td><p>6</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>Listed below</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Excellent class international conference</p></td><td><p>4</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Average-class international conference</p></td><td><p>1-2</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>Case-by-case review and cannot exceed 2 points in total point</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Domestic Conference</p></td><td><p>1-2</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="4"><p>iii. One published case study </p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Harvard Business School Publishing</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Ivey Publishing, Richard Ivey School of Business Foundation</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Kung-Hwa Management Cases Collections</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>Cannot exceed 4 points in total point</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>Taiwan Management Case Center</p></td><td><p>2</p></td></tr></table>

4. The list of Top class international conferences is as below:

<table><tr><td><p>Group</p></td><td><p>Top-class international conference</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Management </p></td><td><ul><li>Academy of Management (AOM) Annual Meeting </li><li>ACR North American Conference </li><li>International Conference on Information Systems (ICIS)</li><li>American Finance Association Annual Meeting/American Economic Association Annual Meeting (AFA/AEA)</li><li>Western Finance Association Annual Meeting (WFA)</li><li>Financial Management Association Annual Meeting (FMA)</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><ul><li>American Finance Association Annual Meeting/American Economic Association Annual Meeting (AFA/AEA)</li><li>Western Finance Association Annual Meeting (WFA)</li><li>Financial Management Association Annual Meeting (FMA)</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><p>Accounting</p></td><td><ul><li>AAA Annual Meeting</li><li>AAA Regional Meeting</li><li>AAA Section Meeting</li><li>Financial Management Association Annual Meeting (FMA)</li><li>American Finance Association Annual Meeting/American Economic Association Annual Meeting (AFA/AEA)</li></ul></td></tr></table>

5. List of Excellent class international conference is as below:

<table><thead><tr><th><p>Group</p></th><th><p>Excellent class international conference </p></th></tr><tr><th><p>Management</p></th><th><ul><li>Academy of Human Resource Development Annual Meeting </li><li>Asia Academy of Management Annual Meeting (AAOM) </li><li>Australia and New Zealand International Business Academy (ANZIBA) Annual Conference</li><li>Australian and New Zealand Academy of Management Conference (ANZAM) </li><li>British Academy of Management Conference (BAM) </li><li>Eastern Academy of Management Annual Meeting </li><li>EGOs Colloquium </li><li>European Association of Work and Organizational Psychology</li><li>International Labor and Employment Relations Association (ILERA) Asian Congress </li><li>International Labor and Employment Relations Association (ILERA) Biannual Congress</li><li>International Association for Chinese Management Research (IACMR) </li><li>International Association for Conflict Management (IACM) Annual Conference</li><li>International Conference on HRD Research and Practice Across Europe </li><li>Labor and Employment Relations Association (LERA) Annual Meeting  </li><li>Midwest Academy of Management Annual Meeting </li><li>Northeast Decision Sciences Institute Annual Conference (NEDSI) </li><li>Society for Industrial &amp; <table><thead><tr><th></th><th><ul><li>Asian Meeting of the Econometric Society</li><li>SoFiE Annual Conference</li><li>International Symposium on Econometric Theory and Applications (SETA)</li><li>PICMET( Portland International Center for Management of Engineering and Technology)</li><li>Or other equivalent-quality international conference approved by finance group faculty</li></ul></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><p>Finance</p></td><td><ul><li>EFA (European Finance Association Meeting) </li><li>EFMA (European Financial Management Association Meeting) </li><li>Financial Management Association (FMA) Asian Conference</li><li>Financial Management Association (FMA) European Conference</li><li>North American Meeting of the Econometric Society Research Symposium (GMARS)</li><li>SoFiE Annual Conference</li><li>International Symposium on Econometric Theory and Applications (SETA)</li><li>Or other equivalent-quality international conference approved by finance group faculty</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table>

6.	Students should publish papers with oral presentations at conferences and should present in English at international conferences. Only the presenter's paper can be counted as a pointed publication. If there are any other Ph.D. students who co-write the paper with you, you would need to fill in the “Quitclaim of Co-authored Dissertation” as attachment 10 with all the co-author signatures on it.

7.	Similar content articles published in different conferences can only be counted in higher points once reviewed by program committee meetings.

8.	Definition of "one periodical article":

1. Articles with one to four authors (at least one of them must be an assistant professor or above in the College of Management, YZU) can be counted as one publication.
2. Articles with five to seven authors (at least three of them must be assistant professors or above and two of them must be assistant professors or above in the College of Management, YZU) can be counted as one-half publication only.
3. Articles with eight authors or above cannot be considered as pointed publications.
4. For Articles with two students or above as authors, the point will be counted on average.

6. Dissertation Oral Defense

Students should follow the procedure of the dissertation oral defense application along with the school calendar. The application documents include:

- Draft of dissertation
- Dissertation Recognition from Advisor (as Attachment 5)
- Checklist for Applying Dissertation Oral Defense (as Attachment 8)

The committee members will work out an average score. The passing score is 70 out of 100. Students who fail the oral defense may apply for another oral defense in the next semester with a limitation of a one-time chance.

Students who have already applied for dissertation oral defense but cannot execute the defense should submit a "Notification of Withdrawal of Application for Examination" (as Attachment 6) to withdraw the defense before the deadline for dissertation oral defense. The withdrawal of oral defense can only be applied for one time. Students who do not submit the form of “Notification of Withdrawal of Application for Examination” and do not execute the defense will be considered as a failure of the oral defense.

Students could appeal to the Ph.D. program when they reach the final year of the Ph.D. study period and are qualified to apply for oral defense but still cannot get the approval to execute the oral defense from their dissertation advisors.

In the event that the program confers a degree to a student who is found upon investigation to have committed plagiarism or used fraudulent means in preparing the dissertation, the program shall revoke the degree and issue a public notice to announce the invalidation of the previously issued diploma.

2. Anything this study guide has not stated clearly, please refer to the relevant regulations of YZU.

To complete the doctoral program, students must earn at least 18 credits within the college and complete a doctoral dissertation.</p><p>2. Additional required courses:</p><p>  For the Management major, students must take "Strategic Theory and Management" and "Behavioral Science Theory and Management."</p><p>  For the Finance major, students must take "Financial Theory" and "Econometrics."</p><p>  For the Accounting major, students must take "Financial Accounting Theory" and "Econometrics."</p><p>3. For matters related to these requirements, please refer to the college’s "Doctoral Program Study Guidelines" and relevant regulations.</p><p>4. Incoming graduate students must complete the Academic Research Ethics Education Course, as outlined in the university's implementation guidelines, by the end of their first semester. At the latest, students must complete the course before applying for the degree oral examination, students who do not complete the course may not apply for the oral defense.</p></td></tr></table>

```markdown
元智大學管理學院博士班學術組修業要點

（111學年度入學學生適用）

111.04.20 一一○學年度第六次教務會議通過

111.11.16 一一一學年度第二次教務會議通過

112.05.31 一一一學年度第七次教務會議修訂通過

# 總則

### 本修業要點依元智大學碩、博士班研究生學位考試細則訂定之。

### 元智大學管理學院博士班(本要點稱本博士班)設有學術組(本要點稱本組)及產業組。

# 修業年限及學分規定

第三條   修業年限

博士班修業年限為二至七年。

第四條  學分數及必選修科目

- 博士生需在本博士班至少修滿十八學分及完成博士論文乙篇。
- 本組修習之科目包括：

1. 基礎必修(3學分)：「社會科學研究方法」
2. 其他必修(6學分)：「策略理論與管理」、「行為科學理論與管理」、「財務與會計理論」三選二。

3.其它選修科目：請參照博士班修業規定之選修科目表。非表列之管理相關領域，需在導師或論文指導教授同意下，提出選修科目表，送班務會議通過後實施之。

- 本組博士班生於修業前二年內，應選修本班所開設之專題研討課程，該課程不列入畢業學分，並至少在學位論文口試前於專題研討課程中發表論文一次。
- 博士班生於找到指導教授後三年內，應選修本班所開設之獨立研究課程~~，並於修課學期前，投稿至修業要點所列優良或頂尖國際研討會中並獲接受~~。

# 資格考試

- 修習本博士班課程應於規定時間填具「資格考試/論文計畫書申請表」(附件一)，並通過下列考試：

<table><tr><td colspan="3"><p>資格考試說明要點</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>考試時間</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>資格考考試科目</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>每學期至少舉行一次</p><p>(每學期開學前一週舉行)</p></td><td><p>社會科學研究方法</p></td><td><p>策略理論與管理</p><p>行為科學理論與管理</p><p>財務與會計理論</p><p>(三選一)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p></td><td colspan="2"><ol><li>資格考試(含重考)須於在學三年內通過，未能通過者，予以退學。</li><li>資格考試的考試科目修課通過後(70分以上(含))，方可申請。各科目成績獨立計算，及格分數為70分以上(含70分)。</li><li>資格考試不及格者必須重考，不論科目以一次為限，重考未通過者，予以退學。</li><li>資格考提出申請後不得撤銷。如因不可抗拒因素無法前來考試，需於考試日前一週提出撤銷申請，若遇重大事由無法如期提出撤銷申請，得於考試日後一週內補提申請，並經班務會議通過後，得不算不及格，但申請次數以一次為限。</li><li>學生以期刊發表抵免資格考試，抵免注意事項如下:</li></ol><p>(1)申請抵免之期刊必須是SSCI、SCI、TSSCI期刊。</p><p>   (2)申請抵免之期刊論文必須是博士班入學後，以元智大學管理學院名義發表，且需含本院專任教師為共同作者。</p><p>(3)申請抵免之期刊論文，每篇僅能被一名博士生申請抵免，且已抵免之論文不得採計畢業研究點數。</p><p>(4)學生應備妥申請表、論文接受函(已刊登者免)、論文摘要、期刊級別佐證資料向辦公室辦理申請。</p><p>(5)資格考試抵免需於在學三年內完成。</p></td></tr></table>

- 博士學位論文

- 論文指導教授之申請

博士生需於資格考試通過後，就其研究領域填具「論文指導教授申請表」(附件二)向本博士班申請一位或多位論文指導教授共同指導，指導教授應以該主修專任教師為優先，若非該主修專任教師或需找校外老師共同指導，需經該主修召集人同意後報請班務會議核備。在博士生未選定指導教授前，由本博士班指派本院專任教師擔任導師，指導其課業。博士候選人選定題目後，在論文指導教授之指導下，進行論文計畫之寫作。

- 指導教授之變更

更換指導教授申請，需與提出論文指導教授申請間隔一學期，亦即不得在同一學期提出申請。博士生應填具「更換論文指導教授申請表」(附件三)辦理，並提出原論文指導教授與新的指導教授之同意書，經班務會議通過後變更。更換論文指導教授與提出論文計畫書口試及學位論文口試申請不能為同一學期，且更換論文指導教授以一次為原則，並需經班務會議通過，博士生未依規定逕自更換指導教授時，其學位考試成績不予承認。

- 指導關係之終止

若因故需終止指導關係，可由指導老師或學生方，依規定主動提出申請，並經班務會議討論通過。通過後學生需重新申請指導教授。

- 論文考試委員會

博士生得於博三上開始提出論文考試申請，並組成論文考試委員會。該委員會負責學位論文之口試，委員由指導教授提名並經該主修召集人及本博士班班主任同意後，聘請相關領域學者五至九人組成之。其中教授或副教授委員應至少佔委員會人數一半以上，校外委員至少佔論文考試委員會一半人數，且扣除指導教授後，應至少含該主修教師一名，考試時由委員會互推一人擔任主席。考試委員名單若有變動，需重新送交「論文考試委員會名冊」(附件四)辦理相關事宜。

為博士生三等親以內親屬或重大利害關係人，應自行迴避不得擔任該生之指導教授或論文考試委員，經發現者撤銷其資格，如已完成口試，則該次口試成績無效。已授予博士學位始發現時，則撤銷其學位，並追繳其已發之學位證書。

- 論文計畫書口試

申請時應填具(1)論文計畫書口試申請表(附件一)、(2)論文考試委員會名冊(附件四)、(3) 歷年成績單與(4)論文計畫書口試檢查表(附件七)，經指導教授及該主修召集人同意後報請班務會議核備。口試由該生論文考試委員會中之校內委員出席。口試成績以七十分為及格，一百分為滿分，以出席委員評定分數平均決定之。論文計畫書口試與學位論文口試不能為同一學期。<u>若通過論文計畫書口試當學期辦理休學，需於復學後重新申請，再進行一次論文計畫書口試。博七上學期結束前未通過論文計畫書口試者，予以退學。</u>

- 研究成果發表

- 學生需與指導教授合著論文，研究機構為元智大學，並為就讀本博士班就學期間所發表。
- 6點以上即符合研究成果發表之要求。除修業年限最後一年（博七）的學生之外，畢業研究成果發表點數，僅採計期刊論文點數。
- 所有相關成果發表之內涵須與管理專業領域契合，投稿前需先經指導教授審核並同意。「其他具匿名審查制之英文期刊（及其計點）」、「其他國際或國內學術研討會(及其計點)」之範圍，須事先申請由各主修召集人審定，並經班務會議備查。
- 頂尖國際研討會，會議名稱如下表。

- 研討會須以口頭報告方式發表，國際研討會論文須以英文發表，申請人需為發表人。若有其他博士生合著，需填寫研討會論文採計畢業研究點數申請表，經所有合著博士生簽名同意，方可採計為畢業研究點數。
- 不同成果發表之內涵，若重疊性高，由班務會議審查決定，以較高之點數計分一次。
- 期刊論文乙篇定義：

1. 一至四人合著(其中至少一人須為本院助理教授或以上)，以1篇計算。
2. 五至七人合著(至少三位為助理教授或以上，其中至少二人須為本院助理教授或以上)，以0.5篇計算。
3. 八人以上合著：不計入。
4. 兩位以上學生合著論文，其點數依平均方式計算。

- 學位論文口試

博士生申請博士學位論文口試，應依照行事曆規定時間內申請，申請時應檢齊(1)論文初稿、(2)指導教授推薦函(附件五)與(3)畢業論文口試檢查表(附件八)後報請學校核備。論文初稿需符合管理專業領域，口試成績以七十分為及格，一百分為滿分。博士學位論文口試成績以出席委員評定分數平均決定之。口試不及格者，得申請於次學期再次舉行，但以一次為限。已申請博士學位考試之博士生，若因故無法在該學期內完成學位考試，應於本博士班規定之口試截止日前填具「學位考試撤銷申請書」(附件六)報請撤銷該學期學位考試之申請，撤銷學位口試之申請以一次為限。逾期未撤銷亦未舉行考試者，以一次不及格論。博士生已達修業年限最後一年且符合申請口試資格，仍無法獲得指導教授同意進行學位論文口試，可向本博士班提出申訴。

本博士班對已授予之博士學位，如發現論文有抄襲或舞弊情事，經調查屬實者，則撤銷其學位，並追繳其已發之學位證書。

- 畢業查核項目

下表任一項目未於規定時間內完成者，予以退學

**元智大學　管理學院博士班**

**（Doctor of Philosophy Program, Yuan Ze University）**

**學術組必修科目表**

**（112學年度入學新生適用）**

**List of Required Courses**

**（For foreign students, entrance in academic year 112）**

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

```markdown
元智大學管理學院博士班學術組修業要點

（112學年度入學學生適用）

112.03.16 一一一學年度第四次班課程會議通過

112.03.30 一一一學年度第五次班課程會議通

112.05.31 一一一學年度第七次教務會議修訂通過

# 總則

### 本修業要點依元智大學碩、博士班研究生學位考試細則訂定之。

### 元智大學管理學院博士班(本要點稱本博士班)設有學術組(本要點稱本組)及產業組。

# 修業年限及學分規定

第三條   修業年限

博士班修業年限為二至七年。

第四條  學分數及必選修科目

- 博士生需在本博士班至少修滿十八學分及完成博士論文乙篇。
- 本組修習之科目包括：

1. 基礎必修(3學分)：「社會科學研究方法」
2. 其他必修(6學分)：「策略理論與管理」、「行為科學理論與管理」、「財務與會計理論」三選二。

3.其它選修科目：請參照博士班修業規定之選修科目表。非表列之管理相關領域，需在導師或論文指導教授同意下，提出選修科目表，送班務會議通過後實施之。

- 本組博士班生於修業前二年內，應選修本班所開設之專題研討課程，該課程不列入畢業學分，並至少在學位論文口試前於專題研討課程中發表論文一次。
- 博士班生於找到指導教授後三年內，應選修本班所開設之獨立研究課程~~，並於修課學期前，投稿至修業要點所列優良或頂尖國際研討會中並獲接受~~。

# 資格考試

- 修習本博士班課程應於規定時間填具「資格考試/論文計畫書申請表」(附件一)，並通過下列考試：

<table><tr><td colspan="3"><p>資格考試說明要點</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>考試時間</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>資格考考試科目</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>每學期至少舉行一次</p><p>(每學期開學前一週舉行)</p></td><td><p>社會科學研究方法</p></td><td><p>策略理論與管理</p><p>行為科學理論與管理</p><p>財務與會計理論</p><p>(三選一)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p></td><td colspan="2"><ol><li>資格考試(含重考)須於在學三年內通過，未能通過者，予以退學。</li><li>資格考試的考試科目修課通過後(70分以上(含))，方可申請。各科目成績獨立計算，及格分數為70分以上(含70分)。</li><li>資格考試不及格者必須重考，不論科目以一次為限，重考未通過者，予以退學。</li><li>資格考提出申請後不得撤銷。如因不可抗拒因素無法前來考試，需於考試日前一週提出撤銷申請，若遇重大事由無法如期提出撤銷申請，得於考試日後一週內補提申請，並經班務會議通過後，得不算不及格，但申請次數以一次為限。</li><li>學生以期刊發表抵免資格考試，抵免注意事項如下:</li></ol><p>(1)申請抵免之期刊必須是SSCI、SCI、TSSCI期刊。</p><p>   (2)申請抵免之期刊論文必須是博士班入學後，以元智大學管理學院名義發表，且需含本院專任教師為共同作者。</p><p>(3)申請抵免之期刊論文，每篇僅能被一名博士生申請抵免，且已抵免之論文不得採計畢業研究點數。</p><p>(4)學生應備妥申請表、論文接受函(已刊登者免)、論文摘要、期刊級別佐證資料向辦公室辦理申請。</p><p>(5)資格考試抵免需於在學三年內完成。</p></td></tr></table>

- 博士學位論文

- 論文指導教授之申請

博士生需於資格考試通過後，就其研究領域填具「論文指導教授申請表」(附件二)向本博士班申請一位或多位論文指導教授共同指導，指導教授應以該主修專任教師為優先，若非該主修專任教師或需找校外老師共同指導，需經該主修召集人同意後報請班務會議核備。在博士生未選定指導教授前，由本博士班指派本院專任教師擔任導師，指導其課業。博士候選人選定題目後，在論文指導教授之指導下，進行論文計畫之寫作。

- 指導教授之變更

更換指導教授申請，需與提出論文指導教授申請間隔一學期，亦即不得在同一學期提出申請。博士生應填具「更換論文指導教授申請表」(附件三)辦理，並提出原論文指導教授與新的指導教授之同意書，經班務會議通過後變更。更換論文指導教授與提出論文計畫書口試及學位論文口試申請不能為同一學期，且更換論文指導教授以一次為原則，並需經班務會議通過，博士生未依規定逕自更換指導教授時，其學位考試成績不予承認。

- 指導關係之終止

若因故需終止指導關係，可由指導老師或學生方，依規定主動提出申請，並經班務會議討論通過。通過後學生需重新申請指導教授。

- 論文考試委員會

博士生得於博三上開始提出論文考試申請，並組成論文考試委員會。該委員會負責學位論文之口試，委員由指導教授提名並經該主修召集人及本博士班班主任同意後，聘請相關領域學者五至九人組成之。其中教授或副教授委員應至少佔委員會人數一半以上，校外委員至少佔論文考試委員會一半人數，且扣除指導教授後，應至少含該主修教師一名，考試時由委員會互推一人擔任主席。考試委員名單若有變動，需重新送交「論文考試委員會名冊」(附件四)辦理相關事宜。

為博士生三等親以內親屬或重大利害關係人，應自行迴避不得擔任該生之指導教授或論文考試委員，經發現者撤銷其資格，如已完成口試，則該次口試成績無效。已授予博士學位始發現時，則撤銷其學位，並追繳其已發之學位證書。

- 論文計畫書口試

申請時應填具(1)論文計畫書口試申請表(附件一)、(2)論文考試委員會名冊(附件四)、(3) 歷年成績單與(4)論文計畫書口試檢查表(附件七)，經指導教授及該主修召集人同意後報請班務會議核備。口試由該生論文考試委員會中之校內委員出席。口試成績以七十分為及格，一百分為滿分，以出席委員評定分數平均決定之。論文計畫書口試與學位論文口試不能為同一學期。<u>若通過論文計畫書口試當學期辦理休學，需於復學後重新申請，再進行一次論文計畫書口試。博七上學期結束前未通過論文計畫書口試者，予以退學。</u>

- 研究成果發表

<table><tr><td><p><a></a>研究成果發表類型及項目</p></td><td><p>點數</p></td><td><p>備註</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="3"><p>一、期刊論文乙篇（被接受或發表在下述期刊，分數擇優採認）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>SSCI期刊</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td rowspan="6"></td></tr><tr><td><p>SCI期刊</p></td><td><p>8</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>TSSCI期刊</p></td><td><p>6</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>FLI期刊</p></td><td><p>6</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>ABDC Journal Quality List B級以上</p></td><td><p>6</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>科技部推薦期刊B級以上</p></td><td><p>6</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Scopus database</p></td><td><p><s>4</s></p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>其他具匿名審查制之英文期刊</p></td><td><p>3-4</p></td><td><p>逐案審定</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="3"><p>二、研討會發表乙篇</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>頂尖國際研討會</p></td><td><p>6</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>正面表列</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>優良國際研討會</p></td><td><p>4</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>優良國際研討會之博士生論壇(PDW)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>其他國際或國內學術研討會</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>1-2</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>逐案審定且總分不得超過2點</p></td></tr><tr></tr><tr><td colspan="3"><p>三、個案發表乙篇</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Harvard Business School Publishing</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>Ivey Publishing, Richard Ivey School of Business Foundation</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>光華管理個案收錄庫</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>總分不得超過4點</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>台灣管理個案中心（哈佛）</p></td><td><p>2</p></td></tr></table>

- 學生需與指導教授合著論文，研究機構為元智大學，並為就讀本博士班就學期間所發表。
- 6點以上即符合研究成果發表之要求。除修業年限最後一年（博七）的學生之外，畢業研究成果發表點數，僅採計期刊論文點數。
- 所有相關成果發表之內涵須與管理專業領域契合，投稿前需先經指導教授審核並同意。「其他具匿名審查制之英文期刊（及其計點）」、「其他國際或國內學術研討會(及其計點)」之範圍，須事先申請由各主修召集人審定，並經班務會議備查。
- 頂尖國際研討會，會議名稱如下表。

Conference (Europe)</li><li>European Marketing Academy Conference (EMAC)</li><li>Frontiers in Service Conference</li><li>Informs Marketing Science Society Conference</li><li>Summer Society of Consumer Psychology (SCP) Conference (Division 23 of APA)</li><li>European International Business Academy(EIBA) Annual Conference</li><li>Industry Studies Conference(ISC) </li><li>R&amp;D Management Conference( RADMA) </li><li>The Institute for Operations Research and the Management Sciences (INFORMS) Annual Meeting</li><li>The Production and Operations Management Society (POMS) Annual Conference Society of Consumer Psychology Conference</li><li>Portland International Center for Management of Engineering and Technology(PICMET)</li><li>International Conference on Management of Technology(IAMOT)</li><li>European Financial Management Association Meeting(EFMA) </li><li>Financial Management Association (FMA) Asian Conference</li><li>Financial Management Association (FMA) European Conference </li><li>North American Meeting of the Econometric Society </li><li>European Meeting of the Econometric Society</li><li>Asian Meeting of the Econometric Society</li><li>The Society for Financial Econometrics (SoFiE) </li><li>International Symposium on Econometric Theory and Applications (SETA)</li><li>Midwest Finance Association Annual Meeting (MFA)</li><li>Asian Finance Association Conference (Asian FA )</li><li>Southern Finance Association Annual Meeting (SFA)</li><li>Asia-Pacific Conference on International Accounting Issues</li><li>Annual Global Management Accounting Research Symposium (GMARS)</li><li>Accounting and Finance Association of Australia and New Zealand (AFAANZ) Conference</li><li>MIT Asia Conference in Accounting </li><li>ABO Research Conference </li><li>ATA Midyear Meetings and JATA Conference</li><li>AAA-AIET Section Mid-Year Conference </li><li>Annual Auditing Midyear Conference, AMC</li><li>Annual Financial Accounting and Reporting Section Midyear Conference</li><li>AAA-IS Section Mid-Year Conference</li><li>Annual IAS Midyear Conference </li><li>MAS  Research  Conference  and  Case  Symposium(MAS Mid-year Meeting) </li></ol><p>或經本主修教師核可同意之優良國際會議及或科技部公告之優良國際會議</p></td></tr></table>

- 研討會須以口頭報告方式發表，國際研討會論文須以英文發表，申請人需為發表人。若有其他博士生合著，需填寫研討會論文採計畢業研究點數申請表，經所有合著博士生簽名同意，方可採計為畢業研究點數。
- 不同成果發表之內涵，若重疊性高，由班務會議審查決定，以較高之點數計分一次。
- 期刊論文乙篇定義：

1. 一至四人合著(其中至少一人須為本院助理教授或以上)，以1篇計算。
2. 五至七人合著(至少三位為助理教授或以上，其中至少二人須為本院助理教授或以上)，以0.5篇計算。
3. 八人以上合著：不計入。
4. 兩位以上學生合著論文，其點數依平均方式計算。

- 學位論文口試

博士生申請博士學位論文口試，應依照行事曆規定時間內申請，申請時應檢齊(1)論文初稿、(2)~~指導教授推薦函(附件五)與(3)~~ 畢業論文口試檢查表(附件八)後報請學校核備。論文初稿需符合管理專業領域，口試成績以七十分為及格，一百分為滿分。博士學位論文口試成績以出席委員評定分數平均決定之。口試不及格者，得申請於次學期再次舉行，但以一次為限。已申請博士學位考試之博士生，若因故無法在該學期內完成學位考試，應於本博士班規定之口試截止日前填具「學位考試撤銷申請書」(附件六)報請撤銷該學期學位考試之申請，撤銷學位口試之申請以一次為限。逾期未撤銷亦未舉行考試者，以一次不及格論。博士生已達修業年限最後一年且符合申請口試資格，仍無法獲得指導教授同意進行學位論文口試，可向本博士班提出申訴。

本博士班對已授予之博士學位，如發現論文有抄襲或舞弊情事，經調查屬實者，則撤銷其學位，並追繳其已發之學位證書。

- 畢業查核項目

下表任一項目未於規定時間內完成者，予以退學

註：採計點數之國際研討會注意事項

1. 需由學術機構或學會主辦，單位內有具名之主席及委員等成員。
2. 研討會需有匿名審稿機制，<strong><u>學生申請時需提供匿名審查意見</u></strong>。

110/1/8

元智大學 管理學院 博士班
